<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">FIFA World Cup hosts</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:502px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:World_cup_hosts.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="643" data-file-width="1461" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/World_cup_hosts.png/500px-World_cup_hosts.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/World_cup_hosts.png/750px-World_cup_hosts.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/World_cup_hosts.png/1000px-World_cup_hosts.png 2x" width="500"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:World_cup_hosts.png" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Map of FIFA World Cup final hosts, 1930–2014. Dark green: twice; middle green: once; light green: planned until 2022</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Sixteen countries have been <b><a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cup</a> hosts</b> in the competition's twenty tournaments since the inaugural World Cup in <a href="/wiki/1930_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1930 FIFA World Cup">1930</a>. The organization was at first awarded to countries at meetings of <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a>'s congress. The choice of location was controversial in the earliest tournaments, given the three-week boat journey between South America and Europe, the two centres of strength in football at the time.</p>
<p>The decision to hold the first cup in <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a>, for example, led to only four European nations competing.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> The next two World Cups were both held in Europe. The decision to hold the second of these, the <a href="/wiki/1938_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1938 FIFA World Cup">1938 FIFA World Cup</a>, in France was controversial, as the American countries had been led to understand that the World Cup would rotate between the two continents.</p>
<p>Both <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a> and <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a> thus boycotted the tournament.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> The first tournament following <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>, held in Brazil in <a href="/wiki/1950_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1950 FIFA World Cup">1950</a>, had three teams withdrawing due to either financial problems or disagreements with the organization.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup></p>
<p>To avoid any future boycotts or controversy, FIFA began a pattern of alternation between the Americas and Europe, which continued until the <a href="/wiki/2002_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2002 FIFA World Cup">2002 FIFA World Cup</a> which took place in Asia. The system evolved so that the host country is now chosen in a vote by FIFA's Council (former Executive Committee). This is done under an <a href="/wiki/Exhaustive_ballot" title="Exhaustive ballot">exhaustive ballot</a> system. The decision is currently made roughly seven years in advance of the tournament, though the hosts for the <a href="/wiki/2022_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2022 FIFA World Cup">2022</a> tournament were chosen at the same time as those for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018</a> tournament.</p>
<p>Only Mexico, Italy, France, Germany (<a href="/wiki/West_Germany" title="West Germany">West Germany</a> until shortly after the 1990 World Cup) and Brazil have hosted the event on two occasions. <a href="/wiki/Mexico_City" title="Mexico City">Mexico City</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Estadio_Azteca" title="Estadio Azteca">Estadio Azteca</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maracan%C3%A3_(stadium)" title="Maracanã (stadium)">Maracanã</a> are the only venues ever to have hosted two FIFA World Cup finals. Only the <a href="/wiki/2002_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2002 FIFA World Cup">2002 FIFA World Cup</a> had more than one host, being split between Japan and South Korea.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1930_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/1930_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1930 FIFA World Cup">1930 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: 1930 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1200" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Hungary" title="Hungary">Hungary</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1500" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="750" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1600" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/23px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/35px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/46px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Uruguay.svg/23px-Flag_of_Uruguay.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Uruguay.svg/35px-Flag_of_Uruguay.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Uruguay.svg/45px-Flag_of_Uruguay.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Before the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Congress" title="FIFA Congress">FIFA Congress</a> could vote on the first-ever World Cup host, a series of withdrawals led to the election of Uruguay; The Netherlands and Hungary withdrew; this was followed by Sweden withdrawing in favour of Italy; then both Italy and Spain withdrew, in favour of the only remaining candidate Uruguay. The FIFA Congress met in <a href="/wiki/Barcelona" title="Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, Spain on 18 May 1929 to ratify the decision, and Uruguay was chosen without a vote.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2014)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>Results:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Uruguay.svg/23px-Flag_of_Uruguay.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Uruguay.svg/35px-Flag_of_Uruguay.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Uruguay.svg/45px-Flag_of_Uruguay.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a></b></li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1500" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a></s> <i>withdrew</i></li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="750" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a></s> <i>withdrew</i></li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1600" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/23px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/35px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/46px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a></s> <i>withdrew</i></li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a></s> <i>withdrew</i></li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1200" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_Hungary_with_arms_%28state%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Hungary" title="Hungary">Hungary</a></s> <i>withdrew</i></li>
</ol>
<p>Notice that the celebration of the first World Cup coincided with the centennial anniversary of the <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_Uruguay_of_1830" title="Constitution of Uruguay of 1830">first Constitution of Uruguay</a>. For that reason, the main stadium built in Montevideo for the World Cup was named <a href="/wiki/Estadio_Centenario" title="Estadio Centenario">Estadio Centenario</a>.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1934_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/1934_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1934 FIFA World Cup">1934 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: 1934 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1500" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1600" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/23px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/35px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/46px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Sweden decided to withdraw before the vote, allowing the only remaining candidate Italy to take the hosting job for the 1934 World Cup. The decision was ratified by the FIFA Congress in <a href="/wiki/Stockholm" title="Stockholm">Stockholm</a>, Sweden and <a href="/wiki/Z%C3%BCrich" title="Zürich">Zürich</a>, Switzerland on 14 May 1932. The <a href="/wiki/Italian_Football_Federation" title="Italian Football Federation">Italian Football Federation</a> accepted the hosting duties on 9 October 1932.</p>
<p>Results:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1500" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_Italy_%281861-1946%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a></b></li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1600" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/23px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/35px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/46px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a></s> <i>withdrew</i></li>
</ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1938_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/1938_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1938 FIFA World Cup">1938 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 1938 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany"><img alt="Nazi Germany" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> Germany</li>
</ul>
<p>Without any nations withdrawing their bids before the vote, the FIFA Congress convened in <a href="/wiki/Berlin" title="Berlin">Berlin</a>, Germany on 13 August 1936 to decide the next host of the World Cup. Electing France took only one ballot, as France had more than half of the votes in the first round.</p>
<p>Results:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a></b>, 19 votes</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>, 4 votes</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany"><img alt="Nazi Germany" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> Germany, 0 votes</li>
</ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Cancelled_FIFA_World_Cups_1942_and_1946">Cancelled FIFA World Cups 1942 and 1946</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Cancelled FIFA World Cups 1942 and 1946">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids for 1942:</p>
<ul>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a></s></li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="504" data-file-width="720" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg/22px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg/33px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg/43px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg.png 2x" width="22"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a></s></li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany"><img alt="Nazi Germany" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_German_Reich_%281935%E2%80%931945%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> Germany</s></li>
</ul>
<p>Cancelled election of the host due to the outbreak of the Second World War in September 1939.</p>
<p>Bids for 1946:</p>
<ul>
<li><i>none</i></li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1950_and_1954_FIFA_World_Cups"><a href="/wiki/1950_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1950 FIFA World Cup">1950</a> and <a href="/wiki/1954_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1954 FIFA World Cup">1954 FIFA World Cups</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 1950 and 1954 FIFA World Cups">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1949_bid">1949 bid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 1949 bid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Bid:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="504" data-file-width="720" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg/22px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg/33px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg/43px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg.png 2x" width="22"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Brazil, Argentina, and Germany had official bid for the 1942 World Cup, but the Cup was cancelled after the outbreak of World War II. The 1950 World Cup was originally scheduled for 1949, but the day after Brazil was selected by the FIFA Congress on 26 July 1946 in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Luxembourg_(city)" title="Luxembourg (city)">Luxembourg City</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg" title="Luxembourg">Luxembourg</a>, the World Cup was rescheduled for 1950.</p>
<p>Result:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="504" data-file-width="720" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg/22px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg/33px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg/43px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281889-1960%29.svg.png 2x" width="22"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a></b></li>
</ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1954_bid">1954 bid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 1954 bid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Bid:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1000" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Switzerland.svg/16px-Flag_of_Switzerland.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Switzerland.svg/24px-Flag_of_Switzerland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Switzerland.svg/32px-Flag_of_Switzerland.svg.png 2x" width="16"/>  </span><a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a></li>
</ul>
<p>The 1954 World Cup hosting duty was decided on 26 July 1946, the same day that Brazil was selected for the 1950 World Cup, in Luxembourg City. On 27 July, the FIFA Congress pushed back the 5th World Cup finals for three years, deciding it should take place in 1954.</p>
<p>Result:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1000" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Switzerland.svg/16px-Flag_of_Switzerland.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Switzerland.svg/24px-Flag_of_Switzerland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Switzerland.svg/32px-Flag_of_Switzerland.svg.png 2x" width="16"/>  </span><a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a></b></li>
</ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1958_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/1958_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1958 FIFA World Cup">1958 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 1958 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/1958_FIFA_World_Cup#Host_selection" title="1958 FIFA World Cup">1958 FIFA World Cup § Host selection</a></div>
<p>Bid:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1600" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/23px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/35px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/46px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Argentina, Chile, Mexico, and Sweden expressed interest in hosting the tournament.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-norlin2425_4-0"><a href="#cite_note-norlin2425-4">[4]</a></sup> Swedish delegates lobbied other countries at the FIFA Congress held in <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a> around the opening of the <a href="/wiki/1950_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1950 FIFA World Cup">1950 World Cup finals</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-norlin2425_4-1"><a href="#cite_note-norlin2425-4">[4]</a></sup> Sweden was awarded the 1958 tournament unopposed in on 23 June 1950.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<p>Result:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1600" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/23px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/35px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4c/Flag_of_Sweden.svg/46px-Flag_of_Sweden.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a></b></li>
</ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1962_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/1962_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1962 FIFA World Cup">1962 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 1962 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1500" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/23px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/35px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/45px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/35px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/46px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/West_Germany" title="West Germany">West Germany</a></li>
</ul>
<p>West Germany withdrew before the vote, which took place in <a href="/wiki/Lisbon" title="Lisbon">Lisbon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portugal</a> on 10 June 1956, leaving two remaining bids. In one round of voting, Chile won over Argentina.</p>
<p>Results:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1500" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/23px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/35px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/45px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a></b>, 32 votes</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>, 11 votes</li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/35px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/46px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/West_Germany" title="West Germany">West Germany</a></s> <i>withdrew</i></li>
</ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1966_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/1966_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1966 FIFA World Cup">1966 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 1966 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/23px-Flag_of_England.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/35px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/46px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/35px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/46px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/West_Germany" title="West Germany">West Germany</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="750" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Spain withdrew from the bidding prior to voting by the FIFA Congress, held in <a href="/wiki/Rome" title="Rome">Rome</a>, Italy on 22 August 1960. Again, there was only one round of voting, with England defeating West Germany for the hosting position.</p>
<p>Results:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/23px-Flag_of_England.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/35px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/46px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a></b>, 34 votes</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/35px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/46px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/West_Germany" title="West Germany">West Germany</a>, 27 votes</li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="750" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_Spain_%281945_-_1977%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a></s> <i>withdrew</i></li>
</ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1970_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/1970_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1970 FIFA World Cup">1970 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 1970 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="640" data-file-width="1280" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/46px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="450" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Colombia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Colombia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Colombia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Colombia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Colombia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Colombia.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="700" data-file-width="1000" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/22px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/33px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/43px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png 2x" width="22"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="342" data-file-width="600" height="13" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png/23px-Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png/35px-Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png/46px-Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Peru.svg/23px-Flag_of_Peru.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Peru.svg/35px-Flag_of_Peru.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Peru.svg/45px-Flag_of_Peru.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a></li>
</ul>
<p>The FIFA Congress convened in <a href="/wiki/Tokyo" title="Tokyo">Tokyo</a>, Japan on 8 October 1964. One round of voting saw Mexico win the hosting duties over Argentina.</p>
<p>Results:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="342" data-file-width="600" height="13" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png/23px-Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png/35px-Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png/46px-Flag_of_Mexico_%281934%E2%80%931968%29.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a></b>, 56 votes</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>, 32 votes</li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="640" data-file-width="1280" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/b9/Flag_of_Australia.svg/46px-Flag_of_Australia.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a></s> <i>withdrew</i></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1974.2C_1978.2C_1982_FIFA_World_Cups"><a href="/wiki/1974_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1974 FIFA World Cup">1974</a>, <a href="/wiki/1978_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1978 FIFA World Cup">1978</a>, <a href="/wiki/1982_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1982 FIFA World Cup">1982 FIFA World Cups</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 1974, 1978, 1982 FIFA World Cups">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Three hosts for the 1974, 1978, and 1982 World Cups were chosen in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>, England on 6 July 1966 by the FIFA Congress. Spain and West Germany, both facing each other in the running for hosting duties for the 1974 and 1982 World Cups, agreed to give one another a hosting job. Germany withdrew from the 1982 bidding process while Spain withdrew from the 1974 bidding process, essentially guaranteeing each a hosting spot. Mexico, who had won the 1970 hosting bid over Argentina just two years prior, agreed to withdraw and let Argentina take the hosting position.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1986_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/1986_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1986 FIFA World Cup">1986 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 1986 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bid:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="450" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Colombia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Colombia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Colombia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Colombia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Colombia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Colombia.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Host voting, handled by the then-<a href="/wiki/FIFA_Council" title="FIFA Council">FIFA Executive Committee</a> (or <i>Exco</i>), met in Stockholm on 9 June 1974 and ratified the unopposed Colombian bid.</p>
<p>Result:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="450" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Colombia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Colombia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Colombia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Colombia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/21/Flag_of_Colombia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Colombia.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a></b></li>
</ol>
<p>However, Colombia withdrew after being selected to host the World Cup due to financial problems on 5 November 1982, less than four years before the event was to start. A call for bids was sent out again, and FIFA received intent from three nations:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="1000" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/23px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/35px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/cf/Flag_of_Canada.svg/46px-Flag_of_Canada.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="840" height="13" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/23px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/35px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/46px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="650" data-file-width="1235" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a></li>
</ul>
<p>In Zürich on 20 May 1983, Mexico won the bidding unanimously as voted by the Executive Committee, for the first time in FIFA World Cup bidding history (except those nations who bid unopposed).</p>
<p>Results:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="840" height="13" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/23px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/35px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/46px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a></b> unanimous vote</li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1990_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/1990_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1990 FIFA World Cup">1990 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 1990 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>

<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/35px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/46px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/West_Germany" title="West Germany">West Germany</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="600" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Flag_of_SFR_Yugoslavia.svg/23px-Flag_of_SFR_Yugoslavia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Flag_of_SFR_Yugoslavia.svg/35px-Flag_of_SFR_Yugoslavia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Flag_of_SFR_Yugoslavia.svg/46px-Flag_of_SFR_Yugoslavia.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Socialist_Federal_Republic_of_Yugoslavia" title="Socialist Federal Republic of Yugoslavia">Yugoslavia</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Except Italy and the Soviet Union, all nations withdrew before the vote, which was to be conducted by Exco in Zürich on 19 May 1984. Once again, only one round of voting was required, as Italy won more votes than the Soviet Union.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1994_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/1994_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1994 FIFA World Cup">1994 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: 1994 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="504" data-file-width="720" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg/22px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg/33px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg/43px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg.png 2x" width="22"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/23px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/35px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/45px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="650" data-file-width="1235" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1500" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/23px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/35px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/45px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Despite having three nations bidding for host duties, voting only took one round. The vote was held in Zürich (for the third straight time) on 4 July 1988. The United States won the bid by receiving a little over half of the votes by the Exco members.</p>
<p>Results:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="650" data-file-width="1235" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a></b>, 10 votes</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/23px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/35px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/45px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a>, 7 votes</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="504" data-file-width="720" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg/22px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg/33px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/56/Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg/43px-Flag_of_Brazil_%281968-1992%29.svg.png 2x" width="22"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>, 2 votes</li>
<li><s><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1500" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/23px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/35px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Flag_of_Chile.svg/45px-Flag_of_Chile.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a></s> <i>withdrew</i></li>
</ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="1998_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1998 FIFA World Cup">1998 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: 1998 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/23px-Flag_of_England.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/35px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/46px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/35px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/46px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/23px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/35px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/45px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1000" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Switzerland.svg/16px-Flag_of_Switzerland.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Switzerland.svg/24px-Flag_of_Switzerland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Switzerland.svg/32px-Flag_of_Switzerland.svg.png 2x" width="16"/>  </span><a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a></li>
</ul>
<p>This vote was held in Zürich for the fourth straight time on 1 July 1992. Only one round of voting was required to have France assume the hosting job over Morocco.</p>
<p>Result:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a></b>, 12 votes</li>

</ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="2002_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/2002_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2002 FIFA World Cup">2002 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: 2002 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/23px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/35px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/45px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>/<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="700" data-file-width="1000" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/22px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/33px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/43px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png 2x" width="22"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="840" height="13" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/23px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/35px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/46px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a></li>
</ul>
<p>On 31 May 1996, the hosting selection meeting was held in Zürich for the fifth straight time. A joint bid was formed between Japan and South Korea, and the bid was "voted by <a href="/wiki/Acclamation" title="Acclamation">acclamation</a>", an oral vote without ballots. The first joint bid of the World Cup was approved, edging out Mexico.</p>
<p>Results:</p>
<ol>
<li><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/23px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/35px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_South_Korea.svg/45px-Flag_of_South_Korea.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>/<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="700" data-file-width="1000" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/22px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/33px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/43px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png 2x" width="22"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a></b> (joint bid, voted by acclamation)</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="840" height="13" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/23px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/35px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/46px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a></li>
</ol>
<p>The 2002 FIFA World Cup was co-hosted in <a href="/wiki/Asia" title="Asia">Asia</a> for the first time by <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> and Japan (the final was held in Japan). Initially, the two Asian countries were competitors in the bidding process. But just before the vote, they agreed with FIFA to co-host the event. However, the rivalry and distance between them led to organizational and logistical problems. FIFA has said that co-hosting is not likely to happen again, and in 2004 officially stated that its statutes did not allow co-hosting bids.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FIFAreleaseSA_6-0"><a href="#cite_note-FIFAreleaseSA-6">[6]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="2006_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: 2006 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="504" data-file-width="720" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/22px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/33px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/43px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 2x" width="22"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/23px-Flag_of_England.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/35px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/46px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/35px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/46px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/23px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/35px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/45px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Flag_of_South_Africa.svg/23px-Flag_of_South_Africa.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Flag_of_South_Africa.svg/35px-Flag_of_South_Africa.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Flag_of_South_Africa.svg/45px-Flag_of_South_Africa.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a></li>
</ul>
<p>On 6 July 2000, the host selection meeting was held for the sixth straight time in Zürich. Brazil withdrew its bid three days before the vote, and the field was narrowed to four. This was the first selection in which more than one vote round was required. Three votes were eventually needed. Germany was at least tied for first in each of the three votes, and ended up defeating South Africa by only one vote after an abstention (see below).</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Controversy">Controversy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Controversy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The controversy over the decision to award the <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006 FIFA World Cup</a> to Germany led to a further change in practice. The final tally was 12 votes to 11 in favour of Germany over the contenders <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a>, who had been favorites to win. New Zealand FIFA member <a href="/wiki/Charlie_Dempsey" title="Charlie Dempsey">Charlie Dempsey</a>, who was instructed to vote for South Africa by the <a href="/wiki/Oceania_Football_Confederation" title="Oceania Football Confederation">Oceania Football Confederation</a>, abstained from voting at the last minute. If he had voted for the South African bid, the tally would have been 12–12, giving the decision to FIFA President <a href="/wiki/Sepp_Blatter" title="Sepp Blatter">Sepp Blatter</a>, who, it was widely believed, would then have voted for South Africa.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></p>
<p>Dempsey was among eight members of the Executive Committee to receive a fax by editors of the German satirical magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Titanic_(magazine)" title="Titanic (magazine)">Titanic</a></i> on Wednesday, the night before the vote, promising a <a href="/wiki/Cuckoo_clock" title="Cuckoo clock">cuckoo clock</a> and <a href="/wiki/Black_Forest_ham" title="Black Forest ham">Black Forest ham</a> in exchange for voting for Germany. He argued that the pressure from all sides including "an attempt to bribe" him had become too much for him.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></p>
<p>On 4 August 2000, consequently, FIFA decided to rotate the hosting of the final tournaments between its constituent confederations. This was until October 2007, during the selection of the host for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>, when they announced that they will no longer continue with their continental rotation policy (see below).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="2010_FIFA_World_Cup"><a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=FIFA_World_Cup_hosts&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: 2010 FIFA World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Bids:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Egypt.svg/23px-Flag_of_Egypt.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Egypt.svg/35px-Flag_of_Egypt.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Egypt.svg/45px-Flag_of_Egypt.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a></li>
<li><span style="white-space:nowrap"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="1000" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/Flag_of_Libya_%281977-2011%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Libya_%281977-2011%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/Flag_of_Libya_%281977-2011%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Libya_%281977-2011%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/Flag_of_Libya_%281977-2011%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_Libya_%281977-2011%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Libya_national_football_team" title="Libya national football team">Libya</a></span>/<span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="800" data-file-width="1200" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Flag_of_Tunisia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Tunisia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Flag_of_Tunisia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Tunisia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Flag_of_Tunisia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Tunisia.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/23px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/35px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/45px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="800" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/23px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/35px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Flag_of_Nigeria.svg/46px-Flag_of_Nigeria.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Flag_of_South_Africa.svg/23px-Flag_of_South_Africa.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Flag_of_South_Africa.svg/35px-Flag_of_South_Africa.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/Flag_of_South_Africa.svg/45px-Flag_of_South_Africa.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a></li>
</ul>
<p>The first World Cup bidding process under continental rotation (the process of rotating hosting of the World Cup to each confederation in turn) was the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FIFAreleaseSA_6-1"><a href="#cite_note-FIFAreleaseSA-6">[6]</a></sup> the first World Cup to be held in <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a>. On 7 July 2001, during the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Congress" title="FIFA Congress">FIFA Congress</a> in <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a>, a decision was ratified, which was that the rotation will begin in Africa.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> On 23 September 2002, FIFA's Executive Committee confirmed that only African member associations, would be invited to submit bids to host the 2010 FIFA World Cup.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></p>
<p>In January 2003, <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a> entered the bidding process, but withdrew their bid in September.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup> In March 2003, <a href="/wiki/Sepp_Blatter" title="Sepp Blatter">Sepp Blatter</a> initially said Nigeria's plan to co host the 2010 FIFA World Cup with four African countries would not work.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup> Nigeria had originally hoped to bid jointly with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/West_African" title="West African">West African</a> neighbours <a href="/wiki/Benin" title="Benin">Benin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ghana" title="Ghana">Ghana</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Togo" title="Togo">Togo</a>.</p>
<p>After it was confirmed by FIFA that joint bidding would not be allowed in the future, <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a> withdrew both of their bids on 8 May 2004. On 15 May 2004 in Zürich (the seventh consecutive time that a host selection has been made there), South Africa, after a narrow loss in the 2006 bidding, defeated perennial candidate Morocco to host, 14 votes to 10. Egypt received no votes.</p>
